{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01XVZdSKFLjy5mC3v1xPo3WC","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"I see! So `unknown` is the value from `childValue.IsUnknown()` on line 77, and it's passed to the AddAllSetBlock, AddAllListBlock, AddAllMapBlocks, and AddSingleBlock methods. This marks that a block is unknown.\n\nNow I understand the scenario: when a block is unknown during an update, it will set `UnknownBlocks[key] = true`.
